shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_FORPOL_lead_the_liberation_of_asia
	icon = GFX_goal_chi_international_revolution
	cost = 7

	
	x = 24
	y = 14

	allow_branch = {
		always = no
	}
	available = {
		is_subject = no
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_war = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SZC_FORPOL_lead_the_liberation_of_asia"
		add_political_power = 50
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CHI_found_our_faction_decision
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_FORPOL_we_will_liberate_taiwan
	icon = GFX_goal_reclaim_taiwan
	cost = 3
	relative_position_id = SZC_FORPOL_lead_the_liberation_of_asia
	x = 0
	y = 1

	prerequisite = { focus = SZC_FORPOL_lead_the_liberation_of_asia }
	bypass = { owns_state = 524 }
	will_lead_to_war_with = JAP

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 250
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_war = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_divisions > 99
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			AND = {
				naval_strength_ratio = {
					tag = JAP
					ratio < 1
				}
				JAP = {
					has_war_with_major = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SZC_FORPOL_we_will_liberate_taiwan"
		if = {
			limit = { 524 = { NOT = { is_claimed_by = ROOT } } } #Taiwan
			add_state_claim = 524
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = var:524.owner #Taiwan
			type = take_state_focus
			generator = { 524 }
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0

		}

		}

			factor = 0

				tag = HND

			}

				tag = PRF
				ratio < 2
			}

				tag = RAJ
				ratio < 2
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0

			country_exists = HND
			has_game_rule = { rule = HND_forpol option = HND_FORPOL_CHI }
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SZC_FORPOL_beyond_macmahon_line"
		if = {
			limit = { 858 = { NOT = { is_claimed_by = CHI } } } #Tawang
			add_state_claim = 858
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 897 = { NOT = { is_claimed_by = CHI } } } #Askai Chin
			add_state_claim = 897
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = HND decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = RAJ decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = PRF decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = NEP decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = BHU decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = AFG decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = CEY decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		if = {
			limit = { var:422.owner = { NOT = { tag = CEY } } }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = var:422.owner decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { var:321.owner = { is_indian_tag = no } }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = var:321.owner decision = CHI_liberation_war_decision } #Goa
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.indian_tags_array
				CHI_liberation_war_PREV_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	icon = GFX_goal_construction_engineering
	cost = 3

	relative_position_id = SZC_Industrial_Planning_Committee
	x = -1
	y = 1

	available = {
		SZC_opium_tier_3_unlocked = yes
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Industrial_Planning_Committee
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 5 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Tianfu_Mining_Bureau"
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = SZC_Tianfu_Mining_Bureau
			bonus = 1
			uses = 1
			category = excavation_tech
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_industrial_concern
		show_ideas_tooltip = tianfu_mines
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
}

	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Industrial_Planning_Committee
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 12 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Industrial_Silk"
		add_one_random_civilian_factory = yes
		add_one_random_military_factory = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_aat = no }
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
			show_ideas_tooltip = sichuan_silk
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { mio:CHN_support_equipment_industry_organisation = { is_mio_available = no } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = available_mio_tt
				show_mio_tooltip = CHN_support_equipment_industry_organisation
			}
			mio:CHN_support_equipment_industry_organisation = {
				set_mio_flag = CHN_mio_unlocked
				add_mio_size = 1
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

	}

	ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Xikang_Hydropower"
		601 = {
			if = {
				limit = { dam > 0 }
				increase_state_category_by_one_level = yes
			}
			else = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dam
					level = 1
					province = 4999
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			prioritize_state = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 601 = { dam < 1 } } #separate due to tooltip indentation
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = building_state_modifier|dam
				INDENT = "    "
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		}
		add_one_random_civilian_factory = yes
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

### Shared Military Tree ###
shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
	icon = GFX_goal_break_rifle
	cost = 5

	x = 25
	y = 0

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
			NOT = { has_idea = SZC_internal_divisions }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
			NOT = { has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea }
		}
	}
	offset = {
		x = -1
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Baoding
				has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Officer
			}
		}
	}
	offset = {
		x = -2
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Federalist
		}
	}
	offset = {
		x = -3
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Industrial
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army"
		army_experience = 25
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_XP }
}

### Zhili Military Tree ###
shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_Adopt_The_Southern_Doctrine
	icon = GFX_goal_SZC_southern_doctrine
	cost = 5

	relative_position_id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
	x = 0
	y = 2

	allow_branch = {
		OR = {
			has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Armament
			has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Zhili
			has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Panwenhua
		}
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = SZC_Continue_The_Northern_Doctrine
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_New_Infantry_Weapons
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Recon_Unit_Training
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Mountain_Warfare
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Import_Modern_Artillery
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Adopt_The_Southern_Doctrine"
		add_ideas = SZC_southern_doctrine_1
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_War_Logistics
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_war_in_the_plate
	cost = 5

	relative_position_id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
	x = -1
	y = 4

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Adopt_The_Southern_Doctrine
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_War_Logistics"
		if = { #has better unit org
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_4
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_5 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_5
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_7
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has increased munitions production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has heavy fire tactics and increased munitions production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_10
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_1
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_2
			}
		}
		every_army_leader = {
			add_logistics = 1
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SZC_Heavy_Fire_Tactics
	icon = GFX_goal_GEO_Artillery_Tactics
	cost = 5

	relative_position_id = SZC_Rebuild_The_Sichuanese_Army
	x = 1
	y = 4

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SZC_Asymmetric_Warfare
		focus = SZC_Focus_On_Speed
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed SZC_Heavy_Fire_Tactics"
		if = { #has better unit org
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_3
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_5
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has better unit org and war logistics
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_4
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_7
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has increased munitions production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_6
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_9
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has war logistics and increased munitions production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_8 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_8
				add_idea = SZC_southern_doctrine_10
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has focus on speed
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_2
				add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_5
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has focus on speed and improved army training
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_4
				add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_8
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has increased munitions production
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_6 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_6
				add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_7
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has increased munitions production and improved army training
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_9 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_9
				add_idea = SZC_northern_doctrine_10
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_modify_two_dynmods
				DYNMOD1 = SZC_southern_doctrine
				DYNMOD2 = SZC_northern_doctrine
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					army_attack_factor = 0.1
					tooltip = army_attack_factor_tooltip
				}
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}

				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_2
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_9
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has firepower
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_3
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_10
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has logistics and operations
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_5 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_5
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_12
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has logistics and firepower
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_6 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_6
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_13
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has operations and firepower
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_8
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_14
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has logistics, operations and firepower
			limit = { has_idea = SZC_industrial_army_11 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SZC_industrial_army_11
				add_idea = SZC_industrial_army_15
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = SZC_industrial_army_4
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}

				prioritize_state = yes
			}

			add_one_random_military_factory = yes
		}

	}

			else_if = { #has rural literacy and healthcare
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_social_welfare_13 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_social_welfare_13
					add_idea = SZC_social_welfare_14
				}
			}
			else_if = { #has education reform and healthcare
				limit = { has_idea = SZC_social_welfare_15 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_social_welfare_15
					add_idea = SZC_social_welfare_16
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SZC_social_welfare_3
					add_idea = SZC_social_welfare_4
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH }
	}
